      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 29th century
       </b>
       . During the period 2801 to 2900 there will be 254
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 95 will be partial, 87 will be annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 63 will be total, and 9 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be five, in 2839.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
